# <a name="archived-release-notes-for-semi-annual-enterprise-channel"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-103">有关半年企业频道的已存档发行说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-103">Archived Release notes for Semi-Annual Enterprise Channel</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="dd90f-104">这些发行说明提供了 Office 365 专业增强版、Visio Pro for Office 365、Project Online 桌面客户端和 Office 365 商业版的半年企业频道更新中所包含的新功能和非安全更新的相关信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-104">These release notes provide information about new features and non-security updates that are included in Semi-Annual Enterprise Channel updates to Office 365 ProPlus, Visio Pro for Office 365, Project Online Desktop Client and Office 365 Business.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-105">我们经常会过一段时间就将功能（有时甚至是修补程序）发布到半年企业频道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-105">We often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Semi-Annual Enterprise Channel over a period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-106">即使没有立即看到下述内容，也会很快就能看到的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-106">If you don't see something described below right away, you can expect it soon.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="dd90f-107">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-107">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/when-do-i-get-the-newest-features-in-for-office-365-da36192c-58b9-4bc9-8d51-bb6eed468516)
> - <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-108">如果半年企业频道上的用户从 Office 门户在 Windows 10 上下载并安装 Office 365，则默认情况下不会包括 OneNote 2016。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-108">OneNote 2016 will not be included by default when a user on the Semi-Annual Enterprise Channel downloads and installs Office 365 on Windows 10 from the Office Portal.</span></span>

[//]: # (请勿移除错误详细信息内容结尾)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-115">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-115">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-116">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-116">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-117">此更改通过利用软件呈现避免了某些 Intel 图形驱动程序的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-117">This change circumvents a problem with certain Intel graphics drivers by leveraging software rendering.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-118">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-118">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-119">明年的日历项目在 Outlook 中可能显示错误的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-119">Calendar items for next year may display an incorrect time in Outlook.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="dd90f-120">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-120">Learn More</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/outlook/troubleshoot/calendars/calendar-items-display-incorrect-time)

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-121">解决了导致客户尝试从&quot;错过的对话&quot;消息创建规则时遇到崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-121">Addresses an issue that caused customers to encounter a crash when attempting to create a rule from a &quot;missed conversation&quot; message.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-122">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-122">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-123">修复了与备注页面中打印（某些情况下存在布局问题）有关的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-123">Fixed an issue related to printing in notes page that had layout issues in some cases.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-152">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-152">Resolved issues</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-153">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-153">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-154">解决了导致删除区域后延迟显示键入值的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-154">Resolved an issue that was causing delays in displaying typed values after deleting a range.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-155">解决了一个问题，当创建于早期版本的 Office 中的工作簿在当前版本的 Office 中打开时，可能会导致 Excel 挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-155">Resolved an issue where workbooks created in earlier versions of Office could cause Excel to hang when opened in current versions of Office.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-156">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-156">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-157">解决了导致用户在启用 toast 通知时发现内存泄漏的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-157">Addressed an issue that caused users to observe memory leaks when toast notifications were enabled.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-158">解决了导致用户在 Outlook 中发现内存泄漏的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-158">Addressed an issue that caused customers to notice a memory leak in Outlook.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-159">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-159">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-160">可靠性修复：修复了第三方加载项可能导致 PowerPoint 失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-160">Reliability fix: Fixed an issue where third party add-in might cause PowerPoint to fail.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-161">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-161">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-162">我们修复了在尝试确定某些特殊字符时字体变为 MS Mincho 的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-162">We fixed an issue with font changed to MS Mincho when trying to finalize some special characters.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-163">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-163">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-164">修复了 Win7 中的性能问题，它导致所有应用中功能区内的“插入形状”库大约需要 4 秒钟才会显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-164">Fixed a perf issue on Win7 where the insert shapes gallery from the ribbon in all apps took approximately 4 seconds to appear.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-165">修复了更新后“开始”菜单快捷方式和 Office 文件扩展名会意外消失的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-165">Fixed an issue where Start Menu shortcuts and Office file extensions would unexpectedly disappear following an update.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-166">为了保护 Office 客户的安全，现在仅使用 SHA-2 算法对 Microsoft Office 更新进行签名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-166">To protect Office customers' security, Microsoft Office updates are now signed using the SHA-2 algorithm exclusively.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-172">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-172">Resolved issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-174">解决了一个问题，该问题导致用户（具有除“全部”以外的任何“保持脱机的邮件”设置）在将项目从本地存储移动到 Exchange Online 邮箱的同步窗口之外时发现数据丢失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-174">Addresses an issue that caused users with a "mail to keep offline setting" of anything other than "All" to see data loss when moving items outside of the sync window from a local store to Exchange Online mailbox.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-288">**默认阻止下载 SMIME 加密和签名的电子邮件中的外部内容：** 鉴于 SMIME 协议中的漏洞，Outlook 将阻止下载由 SMIME 加密或签名的邮件上的外部内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-288">**Block download of external content by default in SMIME encrypted and signed emails:** Due to a vulnerability in the SMIME protocol - Outlook will block download of external content on messages that have been encrypted or signed over SMIME.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-289">用户将无法通过 Outlook UI 单击下载外部内容，以防止受到安全漏洞的危害。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-289">Users will not be able to single-click download external content through Outlook UI to protect from the security vulnerability.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-290">“选项”对话框提供了一个新选项，用户可使用它还原至旧行为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-290">There is a new option in the Options dialog to allow for users to revert to old behavior.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-291">**禁用会议转发：** 阻止与会者将会议转发给其他人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-291">**Turn off forwarding for a meeting:** Prevent attendees from forwarding your meeting to others.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-292">只需转到功能区，然后单击“响应选项”即可。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-292">Just go to the ribbon and click Response Options.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="dd90f-293">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-293">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/5C9877BC-AB91-4A7C-99FB-B0B68D7EA94F)
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p121">**日程安排助理中的人员建议：** 安排会议时查看有关要添加的与会者的建议。无需在日程安排助理和收件人行之间来回切换。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/d284c6d9-206e-4926-92b4-5addc0fcbefb)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p121">**People suggestions in the Scheduling Assistant:** See recommendations for attendees to add when you schedule a meeting. No more switching back and forth between the Scheduling Assistant and the To line. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/d284c6d9-206e-4926-92b4-5addc0fcbefb)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-297">**保留会议室变得更加容易：** 使用多个会议室列表查找会议室，切换列表时不会丢失所选的会议室。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-297">**Reserving a room just got easier:** Look for a conference room using more than one room list - and switch lists without losing rooms you've selected.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p122">**重复周期范围的新默认值：** 对于“重复周期”对话框，在过去重复周期范围的默认值为“无结束日期”。这有助于创建长期运行的定期系列，随着时间的推移可能会损坏。我们将“重复周期”对话框的默认值更新为“结束日期”，以便我们的默认值与建议的日历最佳做法相匹配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p122">**New default for range of recurrence:** For the Recurrence dialog, the range of recurrence used to default for "No end date". This facilitated the creation of long-running recurring series, which can become corrupted over time. We are updating the default for the Recurrence dialog to "End by", such that our default value matches recommended best practices for calendaring.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p123">**从“Outlook 提醒”对话框加入团队会议：** 当 Outlook 提醒用户参加即将召开的会议时，如果即将召开的会议是团队在线会议，则它将显示一个“联机加入”按钮。这与从“Outlook 提醒”对话框加入 Skype for Business 会议的体验类似。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p123">**Join Teams meetings from the Outlook Reminders dialog:** When Outlook reminds users of an upcoming meeting, it will show a Join Online button if the upcoming meeting is a Teams online meeting. This is similar to the experience of joining a Skype for Business meeting from the Outlook Reminders dialog.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-303">**停止查看过去活动的提醒：** 可以将日历设置为在活动结束后自动关闭活动提醒。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-303">**Stop seeing reminders for past events:** You can set your calendar to automatically dismiss reminders for events after they've ended.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="dd90f-304">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-304">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/7a992377-ca93-4ddd-a711-851ef3597925)
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-305">**查看安全链接背后的 URL：** 安全链接有助于保护你免受电子邮件中收到的恶意 URL 的攻击，但它们会隐藏原始 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-305">**See the URL behind Safe Links:** Safe Links protects you from malicious URLS received in email but they hide the original URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-306">若要查看原始 URL，请将鼠标悬停在 URL上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-306">To see the original, hover your mouse over the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-307">需要高级威胁防护许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-307">Requires an Advanced Threat Protection license.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="dd90f-308">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-308">Learn more</span></span>](https://products.office.com/exchange/advance-threat-protection)
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-309">**缩放和粘贴：** 选择默认设置用于所有邮件，而无需在每次阅读邮件时调整缩放。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-309">**Zoom and stick:** Instead of adjusting Zoom each time you read a message, choose a default to use for all your messages.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="dd90f-310">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-310">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/56c090bc-e148-44a7-bd06-1290edd38983)
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-311">**邮件加密：仅加密 IRM 策略：** 新的仅加密选项显示在 Office 365 邮件加密用户的“选项”>“权限”菜单中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-311">**Message Encryption: encrypt-only IRM policy:** New encrypt-only option appears in the Options > Permissions menu for Office 365 Message Encryption users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-312">此选项允许你加密邮件并将其发送给组织内部或外部的任何人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-312">This option allows you to encrypt a message and send it to anyone, inside or outside your organization.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-313">**密件抄送 (BCC) 警告：** BCC 信息提示会在你意外对被密件抄送的邮件全部答复之前发出警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-313">**Warning when you've been BCC'ed:** The BCC infotip will warn you before you accidentally reply all to a mail that you've been blind carbon copied on.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-314">**更智能的“收件人:”行：** 在单击“收件人:”行处理邮件时，会提示用户可能要选择的收件人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-314">**A smarter To: line:** When you click the To: line to address a message, we suggest recipients you're likely to choose.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-315">此外，还可以看到收件人的照片，这样用户便能知道自己将要向其发送邮件的收件人是否正确。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-315">Plus, you can see their picture, so you know yo're sending to the right person.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="dd90f-316">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-316">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/147208AF-CA8E-4CDF-B71F-77BA81A54069)
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p129">**能够插入应用了滤镜的 SVG：** Office 用户现在能够插入应用了滤镜的 SVG。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/e2459f17-3996-4795-996e-b9a13486fa79)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p129">**Ability to insert SVG's with filters applied:** Office users now have the ability to insert SVG's that have filters applied to them. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/e2459f17-3996-4795-996e-b9a13486fa79)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-319">**增强了对高清晰度显示器的支持**：现在，如果用户使用多个显示器或笔记本电脑基座配件，Office 应用在每个显示器上都会有清晰画面，即使显示器有不同的缩放设置也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-319">**Improved support for high definition displays:** If you use multiple monitors or a laptop dock, Office apps will now look crisp on every display, even if the displays have different scaling settings.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="dd90f-320">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-320">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/6720ca0e-be59-41f6-b629-1369f549279d)

[Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/e2459f17-3996-4795-996e-b9a13486fa79)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-366">**增强了对高清晰度显示器的支持**：现在，如果用户使用多个显示器或笔记本电脑基座配件，Office 应用在每个显示器上都会有清晰画面，即使显示器有不同的缩放设置也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-366">**Improved support for high definition displays:** If you use multiple monitors or a laptop dock, Office apps will now look crisp on every display, even if the displays have different scaling settings.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="dd90f-367">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-367">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/6720ca0e-be59-41f6-b629-1369f549279d)

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-398">解决了在打开包含使用其规则的名称的条件格式且应用了自定义视图的工作簿时的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-398">A problem that opening a workbook containing conditional formatting that uses a Name for its rule and a custom view is applied has been resolved.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-431">Office 套件：非安全更新程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-431">Office Suite: Non-security updates</span></span>

 - <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-436">解决了 Windows 10 上貌似已清除多位用户的“最近使用的文件”列表这一问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-436">Fixed an issue where the recent files list appeared to have been cleared for many users on Windows 10.</span></span>
 - <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-437">解决了即使站在进行管理器触发的更新，最终用户仍会看到“Office 更新”业务栏的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-437">Fixed an issue that caused an end-user to see an Office Update business bar, even though there is an Admin-triggered update in progress.</span></span>
 - <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-438">解决了与登录提示间歇性空白相关的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-438">Fixed an issues related to intermittent blank sign-in prompts.</span></span>
 - <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-439">修复了以下问题：Office 更新的某些部分不使用传递优化对等缓存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-439">Fixed an issue where parts of an Office update do not use Delivery Optimization peer caching.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="dd90f-440">了解详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-440">Learn more</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/windows/deployment/update/waas-delivery-optimization)
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-441">修复了如果使用 Office 部署工具安装 Office 且存在不匹配的情况时，可能导致产品被删除或未激活的 bug。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-441">Fix to a bug that could lead to products being removed or not activated if Office was installed using the Office Deployment Tool and there was a case mis-match.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-442">修复了导致 Windows 10（版本 1803 或更高版本）设备上出现过多登录提示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-442">Fixed an issue which was causing excessive sign-in prompts on Windows 10 (version 1803 or later) devices.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-443">修复了下载链接图片时导致挂起的回归。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-443">Fixed regression that causes hangs when downloading linked pictures.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-445">修复了版本历史记录解析逻辑中的 bug，这些 bug 在少数情况下会导致文档以只读方式打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-445">Fixed the bug in version history parsing logic that in few cases caused the documents to be opened in read-only.</span></span>

### <a name="excel-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-544">Excel：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-544">Excel: Feature updates</span></span>
 - <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p159">**协作编辑：** 与其他人同时协作处理工作簿。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/7152aa8b-b791-414c-a3bb-3024e46fb104)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p159">**Collaborative editing:** Work with others at the same time in your workbook. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/7152aa8b-b791-414c-a3bb-3024e46fb104)</span></span>
 - <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-547">**云文件“自动保存”功能现已默认启用：** 此更改意味着用户无需担心会丢失对 OneDrive 或 SharePoint Online 上存储的文档所做的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-547">**AutoSave for cloud files is now enabled by default:** This change means users won't have to worry about losing their changes in documents stored on OneDrive or SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span have to explicitly press Ctrl + S or the Save button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-549">但是，他们必须理解这种行为上的变化，以免意外更改文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-549">However, they will have to understand this change in behavior so they don't make accidental changes to documents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-550">请注意，用户可以使用屏幕顶部的“自动保存”切换来关闭“自动保存”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-550">Note that users can turn off AutoSave using the AutoSave toggle at the top of the screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-551">建议你向用户通知即将进行的更改，并让他们了解如何充分利用 Office 365 中的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-551">We recommend that you notify your users about this upcoming change and educate them about how to best take advantage of this new feature in Office 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-552">[了解有关“自动保存”的更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/What-is-AutoSave-6d6bd723-ebfd-4e40-b5f6-ae6e8088f7a5)和[了解有关 IT 管理员应了解的有关“自动保存”的更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/what-it-administrators-should-know-about-autosave-88e0f80f-e5ea-441b-9c5a-259f08490ae7)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span AutoSave](https://support.office.com/article/what-it-administrators-should-know-about-autosave-88e0f80f-e5ea-441b-9c5a-259f08490ae7)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p161">**改进了单元格和编辑栏编辑：** 现可按 Ctrl+A 选择单元格或编辑栏中的文本。同时还改进了对表情符号和其他复杂字符的支持。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/1798d9d5-842a-42b8-9c99-9b7213f0040f)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p161">**Improved cell and formula bar editing:** You can now use CTRL+A to select text in a cell or the formula bar. ### <a name="excel-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-560">Excel：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-560">Excel: Non-Security updates</span></span> 

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-561">修复了以下问题：在合著会话中，当其他用户对切片器中的数据应用列筛选之后，切片器无法正确更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-561">Fixed an issue in coauthoring sessions where a slicer is not properly updated after another user applies a column filter to the data in that slicer.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-562">修复了以下问题：在合著会话中，如果其中一个用户清除了某个切片器的标题，则会导致合著会话中的其他用户遇到 Excel 崩溃的情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-562">Fixed an issue in a coauthoring session where one of the users clears the caption for a slicer and this causes another user in the coauthoring session to experience an Excel crash.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-563">修复了以下问题：将创建的多个表切片器绑定到同一数据列，然后再删除该数据列时，可能会出现崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-563">Fixed possible crash when creating multiple table slicers bound to the same column of data and then deleting that column of data.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-564">修复了以下问题：自动调整列宽选项关闭时，如果刷新单元格中包含换行文本的已筛选查询表，Excel 有时会发生崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-564">Fixed an issue where Excel would sometimes crash while refreshing a filtered query table that contains wrapped text in cells when the option to automatically adjust column widths was off.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-565">修复了以下问题：当切片器中显示的项数改变时，如果在更高版本的 Excel 中打开在 Excel 2007 中保存的切片器，将会触发崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-565">Fixed an issue where slicers saved in Excel 2007 can trigger a crash when opened in newer versions of Excel if the number of items shown in the slicer changes.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-566">引入了对“获取诊断”按钮的支持，以简化对支持请求的调查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-566">Introduces support for the Get Diagnostics button to simplify the investigation of support requests.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-567">已修复以下问题：某些内部版本/版本中不显示 Power Pivot。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-567">Fixed a bug where Power Pivot did not appear in some builds/versions.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-568">已修复 Excel 中的问题：当用户将鼠标悬停在具有许多定义名称的工作簿中的格式化选项上时，Excel 可能无响应，当在选项中禁用实时预览时，Excel 可能在快速分析工具中无响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-568">Fixed the issue in Excel wherein Excel may become unresponsive when the user hovers over formatting options in a workbook with many defined names, and where Excel may become unresponsive in the Quick Analysis tool even when Live Preview was disabled in options.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p164">我们现在正在调查将 Excel 应用程序窗口从一个桌面移动到另一个桌面时性能缓慢的原因。在此期间，如果你发现了此性能缓慢，可以考虑使用以下变通方法：在“文件选项”对话框的“通用”选项卡中，针对“使用多个显示器时”选择“优化兼容性”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p164">We are currently investigating slow performance when moving the Excel Application Window from one desktop to another. In the meantime, if you do notice this slowness then a work around to consider is to select "Optimize for compatibility" for "When using multiple displays" in the "General" tab in the File Options dialog.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-571">已修复以下问题：从图表源数据的原始单元格集更改图表源数据时，Excel 可能出现故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-571">Fixed an issue where Excel may crash when changing a chart's source data from its original set of cells.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-572">已修复以下问题：即使已设置 FullCalcOnLoad 属性，打开时也可能不会进行重新计算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-572">Fixed an issue where recalculation may not happen on open even if the FullCalcOnLoad property is set.</span></span>  
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-573">修复了在日期单元格格式中使用日本和历日历时显示错误年份的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-573">Fixed an issue where the wrong year is shown when Japanese Era calendar is used in date cell format.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p165">将数据导入 Excel 数据模型时，传入的负零值将导致错误。此次修复将此类值导入为零。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p165">When importing data into the Excel Data Model, incoming values of negative zero would result in an error.  The fix imports such values as zero.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-576">修复了以下问题：Excel 数据透视表中的组合（或取消组合）操作有时可能会触发故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-576">Fixed an issue where a group (or ungroup) operation in an Excel PivotTable could sometimes trigger a crash.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-577">修复了制作图表操作可能导致 Excel 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-577">Fixed an issue where charting actions could cause Excel to crash.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-578">修复了对某些用户无意禁用 Power View 加载项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-578">Fixed an issue where the Power View add-in is inadvertently disabled for some users.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-579">修复了在文档恢复期间创建的临时自动恢复文件从未清理的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-579">Fixed an issue where temporary auto-recovery files created during document recovery are never cleaned up.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-580">修复了以下问题：尝试对受保护的工作簿中的文本文件建立新连接时收到“工作簿处于受保护状态，无法更改”的错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-580">Fixed an issue where attempting to make a new connection to a text file in a protected workbook results in getting a "Workbook is protected and cannot be changed" error message.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-581">修复了以下问题：无法快速打印附加到 Outlook 电子邮件的 Excel 工作簿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-581">Fixed an issue where Quick Print of an Excel workbook attached to an Outlook email may not print.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-582">修复了以下问题：单击超链接可能会导致 Excel 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-582">Fixed an issue where clicking on a hyperlink may cause Excel to crash.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-583">修复了以下问题：使用多维数据集函数导致 Excel 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-583">Fixed an issue where using cube functions causes Excel to crash.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-584">Outlook：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-584">Outlook: Feature updates</span></span>
 - <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p166">**辅助功能检查器改进：** 辅助功能检查器已更新了对国际标准与推荐的支持，以使你的邮件更易于访问。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/a16f6de0-2f39-4a2b-8bd8-5ad801426c7f)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p166">**Accessibility Checker improvements:** The Accessibility Checker has updated support for international standards and recommendations to make your messages more accessible. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/a16f6de0-2f39-4a2b-8bd8-5ad801426c7f)</span></span>
 - <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p167">**从配置文件选取器管理配置文件：** 如果启动 Outlook 时使用配置文件选取器，现在可以在无需转到控制面板的情况下进行更改。可通过配置文件选取器进行创建和删除配置文件、更改设置等操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p167">**Manage Profiles from the Profile Picker:** If you use the Profile Picker when Outlook starts up, you can now make changes without going to the control panel. Create and delete profiles, change settings, all from the Profile Picker.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-589">**内置辅助功能：** 通过将说明性可选文字添加到图像，使所有人都可访问你的邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-589">**Accessibility built right in:** Make your messages accessible to everyone by adding descriptive alt text to your images.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p168">**Outlook 加载项警告：** Outlook COM 加载项有时会遇到导致 Outlook 其余部分运行速度变慢的问题。这些问题可能是由事件延迟导致的，例如在 Outlook 文件夹之间切换、新邮件的到达、正在打开日历项目等。出现此类问题时，Outlook 将在通知栏中显示一条警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p168">**Outlook add-in warnings:** Occasionally an Outlook COM add-in can encounter problems that slows down the rest of Outlook. These problems could be due to latency of events such as switching between Outlook folders, arrival of new emails, opening Calendar items, etc. When such issues arise, Outlook will display a warning in the notification bar.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-592">**知道将与谁一起开会：** 即使你不是组织者，现在也可以看到其他人对会议请求的响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-592">**Know who you'll be meeting with:** You can see other people's responses to a meeting request, even if you aren't the organizer.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p169">**绝不错过任何提醒：** 设置在工作窗口中弹出的提醒。如果不设置，Outlook 会在任务栏中闪烁，以引起用户注意。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/7a992377-ca93-4ddd-a711-851ef3597925)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p169">**Never miss a reminder:** Set reminders to pop up over windows you're working in. Otherwise, Outlook will blink in the taskbar to get your attention. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/7a992377-ca93-4ddd-a711-851ef3597925)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p170">**将已删除邮件标记为已读：** 现在可以将任何已删除邮件设置为已读。启用方法为，依次转到“文件”\>“选项”\>“邮件”\>“其他”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p170">**Mark deleted items as read:** You can now set any message that you delete as read. Opt in by going to File \> Options \> Mail \> Other.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p172">**优化创建组的用户体验：** 已优化创建组的用户体验，使其更现代、更简便。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/04d0c9cf-6864-423c-a380-4fa858f27102)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p172">**Refined user experience for creating a group:** We have refined the user experience for the create group to make it look more modern and clutter-free. ### <a name="word-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-670">Word：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-670">Word: Feature updates</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-671">**云文件“自动保存”功能现已默认启用：** 此更改意味着用户无需担心会丢失对 OneDrive 或 SharePoint Online 上存储的文档所做的更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-671">**AutoSave for cloud data-ttu-id="dd90f-672">更改将自动保存到云中，用户将不再需要显式按 Ctrl + S 或“保存”按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-672">Changes will be saved in the cloud automatically, and users will no longer have to explicitly press Ctrl + S or the Save button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-673">但是，他们必须理解这种行为上的变化，以免意外更改演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-673">However, they will have to understand this change in behavior so they don't make accidental changes to presentations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-674">请注意，用户可以使用屏幕顶部的“自动保存”切换来关闭“自动保存”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-674">Note that users can turn off AutoSave using the AutoSave toggle at the top of the screen.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-675">建议你向用户通知即将进行的更改，并让他们了解如何充分利用 Office 365 中的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-675">We recommend that you notify your users about this upcoming change 管理员应了解的有关“自动保存”的更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/what-it-administrators-should-know-about-autosave-88e0f80f-e5ea-441b-9c5a-259f08490ae7)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span AutoSave](https://support.office.com/article/what-it-administrators-should-know-about-autosave-88e0f80f-e5ea-441b-9c5a-259f08490ae7)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p183">**辅助功能检查器改进：** 辅助功能检查器已更新了对国际标准与推荐的支持，以使你的文档更易于访问。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/a16f6de0-2f39-4a2b-8bd8-5ad801426c7f)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p183">**Accessibility Checker improvements:** The Accessibility Checker has updated support for international standards and recommendations to make your documents more accessible. - <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-693">修复了以下问题：创建 Skype for Business 会议期间，终端服务器上运行的 Outlook 冻结。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-693">Fix an issue where Outlook running on terminal server freezes while creating a Skype for Business meeting.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-694">将 EnableRestoreOAuthUsedKeyWhenUsingCachedWebTicket 的默认值更改为 TRUE。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-694">Change the default value of EnableRestoreOAuthUsedKeyWhenUsingCachedWebTicket to TRUE.</span></span>

### <a name="excel-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-868">Excel：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-868">Excel: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p188">**Microsoft Translator：** 使用 Microsoft Translator 将字词、短语或句子翻译成其他语言。可以在功能区的“审阅”选项卡中执行此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p188">**Microsoft Translator:** Translate words, phrases or sentences to another language with Microsoft Translator. You can do this from the Review tab in the ribbon.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-871">**将 SVG 图标转换为形状：** 将所有 SVG 图片和图标都转换为 Office 形状，这样就可以更改它们的颜色、尺寸或纹理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-871">**Convert SVG icons to shapes:** Transform all SVG pictures and icons into Office shapes so you can change their color, size, or texture.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-872">**取消选中单元格：** 在工作表中进行选择，并取消选中不小心单击的单元格，而不必重新开始。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-872">**Deselect cells:** Make selections in your worksheet and deselect cells that you accidentally clicked without having to start over.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-873">**快速访问网站和组：** 使用“文件”菜单处理常用网站和组中存储的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-873">**Quickly access your sites and groups:** Use the File menu to work with documents stored in your frequently used sites and groups.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p189">**数字铅笔：** 使用我们新的铅笔纹理记录或勾画创意灵感。只需倾斜支持的数字铅笔即可绘制底纹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p189">**Digital Pencil:** Write or sketch out ideas with our new pencil texture. Simply tilt to do shading with supported digital pens.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p190">**LinkedIn 功能设置：** 转到“文件”\>“选项”\>“常规”，以控制是否在 Office 应用程序中显示 LinkedIn 功能。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/dc81cc70-4d64-4755-9f1c-b9536e34d381)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p190">**LinkedIn features setting:** Go to File \> Options \> General to control whether LinkedIn features are shown in your Office applications. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/dc81cc70-4d64-4755-9f1c-b9536e34d381)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p191">**3D 模型：** 使用 3D 增强工作簿的视觉效果和创意效果。轻松插入 3D 模型，然后可以在 360 度的范围内旋转它。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/ec5feb79-b0af-47f6-a885-151fcc88ac0a)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p191">**3D models:** Use 3D to increase the visual and creative impact of your workbooks.  Easily insert a 3D model, then you can rotate it through 360 degrees. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/ec5feb79-b0af-47f6-a885-151fcc88ac0a)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-881">**新墨迹效果：** 使用金属笔和墨迹效果（例如彩虹、星系、岩浆、海洋、金色、银色等）以独特的风格表达自己的想法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-881">**New ink effects:** Express your ideas with flair using metallic pens and ink effects like rainbow, galaxy, lava, ocean, gold, silver and more.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p192">**共享文件 UI：** 对于 OneDrive for Business 或 SharePoint 文件，单击功能区右上角的“共享”按钮或依次转到“文件”\>“共享”会启动已简化和改进的“共享”对话框。对于新文件或本地保存的文件，UI 可方便用户将文件轻松上传到 OneDrive，从而开始协作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p192">**Sharing files UI:** For OneDrive for Business or SharePoint files, clicking the Share button in the upper right-hand corner of the ribbon or going to File \> Share launches a simplified and improved Share dialog. For new or locally-saved files, the UI allows users to easily upload their files to OneDrive to start collaborating.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p193">**阻止危险扩展：** 默认阻止激活被视为高风险且作为 OLE 包对象嵌入的扩展。例如，.exe、.vbs 和 .js。[了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/packager-activation-in-office-365-desktop-applications-52808039-4a7c-4550-be3a-869dd338d834)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p193">**Block dangerous extensions:** Extensions that are considered to be high risk, and are embedded as OLE package objects, are blocked, by default, from activating. For example, .exe, .vbs, and .js. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/packager-activation-in-office-365-desktop-applications-52808039-4a7c-4550-be3a-869dd338d834)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p194">**实用的语音提示改进了辅助功能：** 打开音频提示后，可指导用户完成工作。可以在“文件”\>“选项”\>“辅助功能”中找到此功能。不需要加载项。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/49fda9be-cce5-4c72-a87f-b11000197f5f)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p194">**Helpful sounds improve accessibility:** Turn on audio cues to guide you as you work. Find it in File \> Options \> Ease of Access. No add-in needed. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/49fda9be-cce5-4c72-a87f-b11000197f5f)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-891">**按帐户组织的文件位置：** 打开或保存文件时，位置列表是按与位置关联的帐户进行组织。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-891">**File locations by account:** When opening or saving a file, the list of places is organized by the account associated with them.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p195">**触笔自定义：** 选择一组自己的触笔和荧光笔进行墨迹书写。自定义组适用于所有 Windows 电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p195">**Pen customization:** Choose a personal set of pens and highlighters for inking. Your customized set is available on all your Windows PCs.</span></span>

### <a name="excel-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-910">Excel：非安全更新程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-910">Excel: Non-security updates</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-911">修复了在日期单元格格式中使用日本和历日历时显示错误年份的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-911">Fix an issue where the wrong year is shown when Japanese Era calendar is used in date cell format.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p196">将数据导入 Excel 数据模型时，传入的负零值将导致错误。此次修复将此类值导入为零。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p196">When importing data into the Excel Data Model, incoming values of negative zero would result in an error.  The fix imports such values as zero.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-914">修复了以下问题：Excel 数据透视表中的组合（或取消组合）操作有时可能会触发故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-914">Fix an issue where a group (or ungroup) operation in an Excel PivotTable could sometimes trigger a crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-915">修复了制作图表操作可能导致 Excel 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-915">Fix an issue where charting actions could cause Excel to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-916">修复了对某些用户无意禁用 Power View 加载项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-916">Fix an issue where the Power View add-in is inadvertently disabled for some users.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-917">修复了在文档恢复期间创建的临时自动恢复文件从未清理的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-917">Fix an issue where temporary auto-recovery files created during document recovery are never cleaned up.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-918">修复了从 SharePoint Online 打开文件时 Excel 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-918">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when opening a file from SharePoint Online.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-919">修复了以下问题：无法快速打印附加到 Outlook 电子邮件的 Excel 工作簿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-919">Fix an issue where Quick Print of an Excel workbook attached to an Outlook email may not print.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-920">修复了以下问题：单击超链接可能会导致 Excel 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-920">Fix an issue where clicking on a hyperlink may cause Excel to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-921">修复了以下问题：使用多维数据集函数导致 Excel 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-921">Fix an issue where using cube functions causes Excel to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-922">修复了打印或打印预览只打印或显示工作表部分，内容被工作表上的切片器截断的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-922">Fix a problem where print or print preview only prints or displays a portion of the worksheet, with the content being truncated at a slicer on the worksheet.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-923">修复了以下问题：在尝试对受保护的工作簿中的文本文件建立新连接时，收到“工作簿处于保护状态，无法更改”错误消息。修复了以下问题：如果编辑语言为日语、中文或韩语，那么当尝试在“主页”选项卡上选择新字体或进行编辑时，Excel 可能会卡住。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-923">Fix an issue where attempting to make a new connection to a text file in a protected workbook results in getting a "Workbook is protected and cannot be changed" error message.Fix an issue where, if your editing language is Japanese, Chinese, or Korean, Excel may freeze when you try to choose a new font on the Home tab or when you edit.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-924">修复了以下问题：在最小化 Excel 后打开工作簿时，缺少滚动条。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-924">Fix an issue where the scroll bars are missing when a workbook is opened when Excel is minimized.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-925">修复了以下问题：在文件资源管理器中双击文件名打开多个工作簿时，工作簿引用失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-925">Fix an issue where workbook references fail when opening multiple workbooks by double-clicking on the file names in File Explorer.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-926">修复了以下问题：以编程方式依次创建数据透视表和刷新导致 Excel 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-926">Fix an issue where the programmatic creation of a PivotTable followed by a programmatic refresh causes Excel to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-927">修复了以下问题：以编程方式调用 Workbook.Open() 可能会导致 Excel 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-927">Fix an issue where programmatically calling Workbook.Open() may cause Excel to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-928">修复了以下问题：使用宏打开 Office 2007 或更低版本工作簿（.xls 或 .xla）时，用户错误地看到“灾难性故障”错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-928">Fix an issue where the user incorrectly sees a "catastrophic failure" error message when opening an Office 2007 or older workbook (.xls or .xla) with macros.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-929">修复了以下问题：Excel 可能会在用户打开关联菜单时发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-929">Fix an issue where Excel might crash when a user opens a context menu.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-930">修复了以下问题：当用户尝试在现有的工作簿中插入对象时，用户单击“浏览”导致 Excel 发生故障的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-930">Fix an issue where, when the user tries to insert an object in an existing workbook, Excel crashes when the user clicks Browse.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-931">修复了以下问题：如果使用密码保护区域，看不到用于输入密码以解锁区域的对话框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-931">Fix an issue where, when protecting a range with a password, the dialog box to enter the password to unlock the range isn't visible.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-932">修复了以下问题：当文件名包含方括号时，用户无法关闭受保护的视图中的工作簿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-932">Fix an issue where the user can't close a workbook in protected view when the file name contains square brackets.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-933">修复了以下问题：拖动或拖动填充时，工具提示的位置未对齐。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-933">Fix an issue where placement of the tooltip is misaligned when dragging or drag filling.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-934">修复了以下问题：使用“文件”\>“另存为”保存工作簿时，包含句点的文件名在文件保存对话框中显示为空白或被截断。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-934">Fix an issue where, when saving a workbook by using File \> Save As, a file name that contains periods appears blank or truncated in the file save dialog.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p197">修复了以下问题：保存支持同步的文件时，Office 无法写入磁盘，但 Office 仍然将该文件上传到 OneDrive。使用此修复程序后，用户现在将看到一条错误消息，且上传不会继续执行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p197">Fix an issue where, when saving a sync-backed file, Office fails to write to disk, but Office keeps uploading the file to OneDrive. With this fix, user will now see an error message and the upload won't proceed.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-937">Outlook：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-937">Outlook: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-938">**轻松排序电子邮件：** 感谢提供反馈，我们已为未使用重点收件箱的用户，在邮件列表和未读邮件筛选器上方恢复了排序功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-938">**Sort your email with ease:** Thanks to your feedback, we've brought back sorting above the message list and the Unread filter for people who don't use Focused Inbox.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-939">**将 SVG 图标转换为形状：** 将所有 SVG 图片和图标都转换为 Office 形状，以便可更改其颜色、大小或纹理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-939">**Convert SVG icons to shapes:** Transform all SVG pictures and icons into Office shapes so you can change their color, size, or texture.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-940">**Office 365 群组的改进：** 阅读和回复群组对话比以往更加简便，因为可以双击群组消息，在它自己的窗口中打开消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-940">**Improvements to Office 365 groups:** It’s easier than ever to read and reply to group conversations because you can double-click on a group message to open it in its own window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p198">**LinkedIn 功能设置：** 转到“文件”\>“选项”\>“常规”，以控制是否在 Office 应用程序中显示 LinkedIn 功能。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/dc81cc70-4d64-4755-9f1c-b9536e34d381)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p198">**LinkedIn features setting:** Go to File \> Options \> General to control whether LinkedIn features are shown in your Office applications. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/dc81cc70-4d64-4755-9f1c-b9536e34d381)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p199">**3D 模型：** 使用 3D 增强电子邮件的视觉效果和创意效果。轻松插入 3D 模型，然后可以在 360 度的范围内旋转它。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/ec5feb79-b0af-47f6-a885-151fcc88ac0a)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p199">**3D models:** Use 3D to increase the visual and creative impact of your email.  Easily insert a 3D model, then you can rotate it through 360 degrees. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/ec5feb79-b0af-47f6-a885-151fcc88ac0a)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-946">**个人资料卡片：** 无论是桌面版、Web 版还是使用移动应用，都显示与人员和群组最相关的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-946">**Profile card:** Shows you the most relevant details about people and groups, whether you’re on the desktop, the web, or using a mobile app.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-947">**将约会添加到群组日历中：** 现在无需以电子邮件方式发送会议安排，即可让群组中的所有人都知道你何时离开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-947">**Add an appointment to a group calendar:** Now you can let everyone in your group know when you’ll be away without sending a meeting in email.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-948">**下载云附件：** 将 OneDrive 附件保存或拖放到计算机后，我们会为用户下载文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-948">**Downloading cloud attachments:** When you save or drag and drop OneDrive attachments to your computer, we download the file for you.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p200">**实用的语音提示改进了辅助功能：** 打开音频提示后，可指导用户完成工作。可以在“文件”\>“选项”\>“辅助功能”中找到此功能。不需要加载项。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/49fda9be-cce5-4c72-a87f-b11000197f5f)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p200">**Helpful sounds improve accessibility:** Turn on audio cues to guide you as you work. Find it in File \> Options \> Ease of Access. No add-in needed. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/49fda9be-cce5-4c72-a87f-b11000197f5f)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p201">**重点收件箱：** 收件箱分为两个选项卡 – 重点和其他。邮件根据邮件内容以及最常与之交互的联系人进行排序。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/f445ad7f-02f4-4294-a82e-71d8964e3978)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p201">**Focused Inbox:** The Inbox is separated into two tabs – Focused and Other. Messages are sorted based on the content of the message and who you interact with most often. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/f445ad7f-02f4-4294-a82e-71d8964e3978)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-956">**快速访问最常用的组：** 最常与之交互的组现在显示在“文件夹”窗格的“组”下方列表的顶部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-956">**Quickly access the groups you use most:** Groups you're most likely to interact with now appear at the top of the list under Groups in the Folder pane.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-966">Outlook：非安全更新程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-966">Outlook: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-967">修复了切换到发件箱或已发送邮件文件夹会导致 Outlook 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-967">Fix an issue where switching to the Outbox or Sent Items folder causes Outlook to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-968">修复了当会议正文或附件更改时，所有与会者都会收到会议更新（而不是向与会者发送会议更新）属于可选项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-968">Fix an issue where all attendees receive meeting updates when the meeting body or attachments change, instead of sending a meeting update to the attendees being optional.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-969">修复了由于 User-Agent 字符串的更改，导致用户无法连接到 EWS 和 REST 终结点的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-969">Fix an issue that causes users to be unable to connect to EWS and REST endpoints because of a change in the User-Agent string.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-970">修复了以下问题：对与会者更新的会议地点显示旧位置，而不是新位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-970">Fix an issue where a meeting location update to attendees shows the old location instead of the new location.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-971">修复了以下问题：用户在阅读窗格中预览附件时看到错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-971">Fix an issue where the user sees an error when previewing an attachment in the reading pane.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-972">修复了以下问题：在用户撰写电子邮件期间，Outlook 将显示名称解析为电子邮件地址时发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-972">Fix an issue where Outlook crashes when resolving display names to email addresses when the user is composing an email.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-973">修复了以下问题：一些用户没有收到租户管理员已启用的支持功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-973">Fix an issue where some users don't receive support features that have been enabled by their tenant admin</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-974">修复了以下问题：在搜索范围为全部邮箱时，搜索失败且看到“找不到匹配”错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-974">Fix an issue where search fails with “No matches found” when search is scoped to All Mailboxes.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-975">修复了以下问题：如果在使用可访问事件观察程序 (AccEvent.exe) 进行监视时切换文件夹，导致 Outlook 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-975">Fix an issue where, when monitoring using Accessible Event Watcher (AccEvent.exe), Outlook crashes when switching folders.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-976">PowerPoint：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-976">PowerPoint: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p202">**Microsoft Translator：** 使用 Microsoft Translator 将字词、短语或句子翻译成其他语言。可以在功能区的“审阅”选项卡中执行此操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p202">**Microsoft Translator:** Translate words, phrases or sentences to another language with Microsoft Translator. You can do this from the Review tab in the ribbon.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-980">**将 SVG 图标转换为形状：** 将所有 SVG 图片和图标都转换为 Office 形状，这样就可以更改它们的颜色、尺寸或纹理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-980">**Convert SVG icons to shapes:** Transform all SVG pictures and icons into Office shapes so you can change their color, size, or texture.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-981">**修订跟踪信息漫游：** 突出显示其他人修改的共享幻灯片的已读/未读状态，现在存储在漫游服务中（而不是存储在用户本地计算机上），这样就可以跨多个设备或平台同步此类信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-981">**Roaming of revision tracking info:** The read/unread status for highlighting shared slides that have been modified by others is now stored in a roaming service (instead of on the user's local computer) so that this information can be synchronized across multiple devices or platforms.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-982">**快速访问网站和组：** 使用“文件”菜单处理常用网站和组中存储的文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-982">**Quickly access your sites and groups:** Use the File menu to work with documents stored in your frequently used sites and groups.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p203">**数字铅笔：** 使用我们新的铅笔纹理记录或勾画创意灵感。只需倾斜支持的数字铅笔即可绘制底纹。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p203">**Digital Pencil:** Write or sketch out ideas with our new pencil texture. Simply tilt to do shading with supported digital pens.</span></span>

[Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/dc81cc70-4d64-4755-9f1c-b9536e34d381)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p205">**使用数控笔执行幻灯片放映：** 使用 Surface 触控笔或其他带有蓝牙按钮的触笔切换幻灯片。需要安装 Windows 10 Fall Creators Update。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/e36da834-7d34-4b71-aafd-071727549f7a)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p205">**Run a slide show with your digital pen:** Use your Surface Pen, or other pen with a Bluetooth button, to advance your slides. Windows 10 Fall Creators Update is required. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/e36da834-7d34-4b71-aafd-071727549f7a)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p206">**3D 模型：** 使用 3D 增强演示文稿的视觉效果和创意效果。使用切换效果（例如可在幻灯片之间打造电影动画效果的“平滑”）使演示文稿中的 3D 模型栩栩如生。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/ec5feb79-b0af-47f6-a885-151fcc88ac0a)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p206">**3D models:** Use 3D to increase the visual and creative impact of your presentations. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/ec5feb79-b0af-47f6-a885-151fcc88ac0a)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-993">**新墨迹效果：** 使用金属笔和墨迹效果（例如彩虹、星系、岩浆、海洋、金色、银色等）以独特的风格表达自己的想法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-993">**New ink effects:** Express your ideas with flair using metallic pens and ink effects like rainbow, galaxy, lava, ocean, gold, silver and more.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p207">**共享文件 UI：** 对于 OneDrive for Business 或 SharePoint 文件，单击功能区右上角的“共享”按钮或依次转到“文件”\>“共享”会启动已简化和改进的“共享”对话框。对于新文件或本地保存的文件，UI 可方便用户将文件轻松上传到 OneDrive，从而开始协作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p207">**Sharing files UI:** For OneDrive for Business or SharePoint files, clicking the Share button in the upper right-hand corner of the ribbon or going to File \> Share launches a simplified and improved Share dialog. -   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p208">**阻止危险扩展：** 默认阻止激活被视为高风险且作为 OLE 包对象嵌入的扩展。例如，.exe、.vbs 和 .js。[了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/packager-activation-in-office-365-desktop-applications-52808039-4a7c-4550-be3a-869dd338d834)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p208">**Block dangerous extensions:** Extensions that are considered to be high risk, and are embedded as OLE package objects, are blocked, by default, from activating. -   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-999">**修订突出显示：** 突出显示由其他用户已修改的幻灯片。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-999">**Revision highlighting:** Slides that have been modified by other users are highlighted.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1000">**离开期间：** PowerPoint 显示自你上次访问以后对共享演示文稿进行过编辑的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1000">**While you were away:** PowerPoint shows you who edited your shared presentation since your last visit.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1001">**设计器改进：** 现在，设计器会推荐有关项目符号列表中日程表的设计灵感。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1001">**Designer improvement:** Designer now recommends design ideas for timelines in a bulleted list.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p209">**实用的语音提示改进了辅助功能：** 打开音频提示后，可指导用户完成工作。可以在“文件”\>“选项”\>“辅助功能”中找到此功能。不需要加载项。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/49fda9be-cce5-4c72-a87f-b11000197f5f)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p209">**Helpful sounds improve accessibility:** Turn on audio cues to guide you as you work. Find it in File \> Options \> Ease of Access. No add-in needed. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/49fda9be-cce5-4c72-a87f-b11000197f5f)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1006">**按帐户组织的文件位置：** 打开或保存文件时，位置列表是按与位置关联的帐户进行组织。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1006">**File locations by account:** When opening or saving a file, the list of places is organized by the account associated with them.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p210">**触笔自定义：** 选择一组自己的触笔和荧光笔进行墨迹书写。自定义组适用于所有 Windows 电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p210">**Pen customization:** Choose a personal set of pens and highlighters for inking. Your customized set is available on all your Windows PCs.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1009">**设计器改进：** 设计器现在为幻灯片中添加的图表提供设计灵感建议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1009">**Designer improvement:** Designer now recommends design ideas for charts added to your slides.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p211">**快速启动：** 自动生成大纲，帮助用户开始研究他们所选的主题。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/4784f273-0b2c-456c-9c89-24e5b977c224)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p211">**QuickStarter:** Automatically builds an outline to help users get started researching a subject of their choosing. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/4784f273-0b2c-456c-9c89-24e5b977c224)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p212">**数字标尺：** 在具有触摸屏的设备上，转到“绘图”\>“标尺”，然后使用笔或手指绘制直线或对齐一组对象。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/6222c9b4-2fdf-48f7-a3fd-1687fbe2bf84)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p212">**Digital ruler:** On devices that have touch screens, go to Draw \> Ruler, then use your pen or finger to draw straight lines or to align a set of objects. ### <a name="powerpoint-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1014">PowerPoint：安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1014">PowerPoint: Security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1015">[CVE-2017-11934](https://portal.msrc.microsoft.com/zh-CN/security-guidance/advisory/CVE-2017-11934)：Microsoft PowerPoint 信息泄漏漏洞</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1015">[CVE-2017-11934](https://portal.msrc.microsoft.com/zh-CN/security-guidance/advisory/CVE-2017-11934): Microsoft PowerPoint Information Disclosure Vulnerability</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1016">PowerPoint：非安全更新程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1016">PowerPoint: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1017">修复了表格显示不正常并带有粗边框的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1017">Fix an issue where tables are rendered incorrectly with thick borders.</span></span>

### <a name="project-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1031">Project：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1031">Project: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p215">**“任务板”视图：** 在“任务板”视图中，对卡片上的任务进行排序。在任务板上的各栏之间重新排序和移动卡片，就跟在敏捷项目中一样。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p215">**Task Board view:** Sort tasks on cards in the Task Board view. Reorder and move cards between columns on the board just like in Agile projects.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p216">**敏捷项目：** 使用积压工作 (backlog)、任务板、冲刺 (sprint) 等管理敏捷项目。支持使用 Scrum 或看板方法。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/1b9b44d7-fd8e-4b3b-ab94-2b97deb9945b)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p216">**Agile projects:** Manage your Agile projects using backlogs, task boards, sprints, and more. Both Scrum or Kanban methodologies are supported. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/1b9b44d7-fd8e-4b3b-ab94-2b97deb9945b)</span></span>  
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p217">**在规划器中管理任务：** 将项目任务关联到规划器，并为任务创建计划。将任务分解为子任务，添加团队，分配任务，并管理任务板上的工时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p217">**Manage a task in Planner:** Link a Project task to Planner and create a plan for it. Break the task into subtasks, add a team, assign tasks, and manage the work on a task board.</span></span>

### <a name="publisher-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1065">Publisher：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1065">Publisher: Feature updates</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1089">当启用与 Aries 手机和 RedirectClient 配对时，禁止新的呼叫和对话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1089">Suppress new calls and conversations when paired with Aries phones and RedirectClient is enabled.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1090">修复了日期格式不是美国格式 (mm/dd/yy) 时，按日期在 PChat 中搜索消息失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1090">Fix an issue where searching messages in PChat by date fails when the date format is other than US format (mm/dd/yy).</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1091">修复了以下问题：当 EnableExternalP2PFileTransfer 策略设置为 false 时，用户仍能在会议中附加文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1091">Fix an issue where, when EnableExternalP2PFileTransfer policy is set to false, users are still able to attach files in meetings.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p219">修复了以下问题：对话历史记录中显示的是呼叫方，而不是被叫方。如果使用 Active Directory 修改被叫方的工作电话号码，就会出现此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p219">Fix an issue where, in Conversation History, the caller is shown instead of the called person. This happens when the called person's work number is modified using Active Directory.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1094">修复了以下问题：对于向手机号码拨出的传出 PSTN 呼叫，对话历史记录中的呼叫历史记录内缺少接听人信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1094">Fix an issue where, for outgoing PSTN calls to mobile numbers, recipient information is missing in the call history in conversation history.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1095">修复了以下问题：从 Outlook 中的电子邮件启动 IM 时，IM 的主题中没有电子邮件的主题行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1095">Fix an issue where, when initiating an IM from an email in Outlook, the subject line of the email is not included in the subject of the IM.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1096">修复了以下问题：当 IM 对话窗口贴靠到一侧时，对话出现双层堆叠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1096">Fix an issue where, when IM conversation windows are snapped to one side, conversations appear double stacked.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1097">修复了以下问题：在 VDIv2 环境中，VbSS 屏幕共享请求显示为 基于 RDP 的请求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1097">Fix an issue where, in a VDIv2 environment, VbSS screen sharing requests appear as RDP-based requests.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1098">修复了以下问题：当呼叫转移失败时，失败通知中列出的是呼叫方，而不是未接来电的接听人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1098">Fix an issue where, in a failed call transfer, the caller is listed in the failure notification, instead of the missed recipient.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1099">修复了以下问题：客户端升级重定向横幅中隐藏“开始使用 Teams”按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1099">Fix an issue where the "Start using Teams" button is hidden within the client upgrade redirect banner.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1100">修复了以下问题：IM 窗口中的 DPI 缩放问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1100">Fix DPI scaling issues in IM windows.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1101">修复了以下问题：Skype for Business 联系人卡片中不显示 LinkedIn 数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1101">Fix an issue where LinkedIn data does not appear in the Skype for Business Contact Card.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1102">用户现在可以代表智能寻线停止接听电话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1102">Add the ability for users to stop receiving calls on behalf of a hunt group.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1103">如果 Skype for Business 或 Teams 中有通话正在进行中，且接听或启动了新电话，现在可以自动保持呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1103">Add the ability to automatically hold calls when a call is active in Skype for Business or Teams and a new call is received or initiated.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1104">修复了以下问题：用户在共享全屏后无法发送 IM。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1104">Fix an issue where users are unable to IM after full screen sharing.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1105">修复了以下问题：会议厅中的用户在被拒绝进入会议时收不到通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1105">Fix an issue where users in the lobby aren't notified when they're denied from entering the meeting.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1106">修复了以下问题：在通话期间，自动增益控制的增加不受控。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1106">Fix an issue where automatic gain control increases uncontrollably during calls.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1107">修复了以下问题：如果会议室资源邮箱已添加到会议邀请，用户无法在“会议选项”中选择演示者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1107">Fix an issue where users are unable to select a presenter in Meeting Options when a conference room resource mailbox is added to a meeting invite.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1108">修复了以下问题：如果 AllowlPVideo 设置为 False，桌面共享按钮在对等视频呼叫期间灰显。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1108">Fix an issue where the desktop sharing button is dimmed during a peer-to-peer video call if AllowlPVideo is set to False.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1110">修复了以下问题：在聊天窗口中将鼠标悬停在“插入链接”按钮之上时，工具提示不显示，并且在选择此按钮后看不到辅助功能名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1110">Fix an issue where the tooltip isn't shown when hovering over the "Insert Link" button in the chat window, and there isn't an accessibility name when the button is selected.</span></span>

### <a name="word-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1127">Word：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1127">Word: Feature updates</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p229">**LinkedIn 功能设置：** 转到“文件”\>“选项”\>“常规”，以控制是否在 Office 应用程序中显示 LinkedIn 功能。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/dc81cc70-4d64-4755-9f1c-b9536e34d381)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p229">**LinkedIn features setting:** Go to File \> Options \> General to control whether LinkedIn features are shown in your Office applications. -   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p230">**SharePoint 属性面板：** 在文档中显示和编辑 SharePoint 文档库列值。借助“视图”选项卡上的功能区按钮，可以轻松地访问面板，并且 SharePoint 管理员能够使用文档库设置自动打开属性面板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p230">**SharePoint property panel:** Display and edit SharePoint document library column values from within a document. A ribbon button on the View tab provides easy access to the panel and SharePoint admins can use a document library setting to automatically open the property panel.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p231">**3D 模型：** 使用 3D 增强文档的视觉效果和创意效果。轻松插入 3D 模型，然后可以在 360 度的范围内旋转它。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/ec5feb79-b0af-47f6-a885-151fcc88ac0a)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p231">**3D models:** Use 3D to increase the visual and creative impact of your documents.  Easily insert a 3D model, then you can rotate it through 360 degrees. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/ec5feb79-b0af-47f6-a885-151fcc88ac0a)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1143">**新墨迹效果：** 使用金属笔和墨迹效果（例如彩虹、星系、岩浆、海洋、金色、银色等）以独特的风格表达自己的想法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1143">**New ink effects:** Express your ideas with flair using metallic pens and ink effects like rainbow, galaxy, lava, ocean, gold, silver and more.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p232">**共享文件 UI：** 对于 OneDrive for Business 或 SharePoint 文件，单击功能区右上角的“共享”按钮或依次转到“文件”\>“共享”会启动已简化和改进的“共享”对话框。对于新文件或本地保存的文件，UI 可方便用户将文件轻松上传到 OneDrive，从而开始协作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p232">**Sharing files UI:** For OneDrive for Business or SharePoint files, clicking the Share button in the upper right-hand corner of the ribbon or going to File \> Share launches a simplified and improved Share dialog. -   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p233">**阻止危险扩展：** 默认阻止激活被视为高风险且作为 OLE 包对象嵌入的扩展。例如，.exe、.vbs 和 .js。[了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/packager-activation-in-office-365-desktop-applications-52808039-4a7c-4550-be3a-869dd338d834)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p233">**Block dangerous extensions:** Extensions that are considered to be high risk, and are embedded as OLE package objects, are blocked, by default, from activating. -   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p234">**使用学习工具进行编辑：** 学习工具现适用于 Word 的 Web 布局。编辑时，可以调整文字间距，并显示音节。在任意视图中，大声朗读文档时，每个单词都会突出显示。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/a857949f-c91e-4c97-977c-a4efcaf9b3c1)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p234">**Edit using Learning Tools:** Learning Tools is now available in Word's Web Layout. -   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1153">**LaTeX 语法：** 使用 LaTeX 语法创建和编辑数学公式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1153">**LaTeX syntax:** Create and edit math equations using LaTeX syntax.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p235">**实用的语音提示改进了辅助功能：** 打开音频提示后，可指导用户完成工作。可以在“文件”\>“选项”\>“辅助功能”中找到此功能。不需要加载项。 [了解更多](https://support.office.com/article/49fda9be-cce5-4c72-a87f-b11000197f5f)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p235">**Helpful sounds improve accessibility:** Turn on audio cues to guide you as you work. -   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1158">**按帐户组织的文件位置：** 打开或保存文件时，位置列表是按与位置关联的帐户进行组织。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1158">**File locations by account:** When opening or saving a file, the list of places is organized by the account associated with them.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p236">**触笔自定义：** 选择一组自己的触笔和荧光笔进行墨迹书写。自定义组适用于所有 Windows 电脑。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p236">**Pen customization:** Choose a personal set of pens and highlighters for inking. -   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p237">**通过“编辑器”窗格增强了书写帮助：** “编辑器”窗格可用于提供高级拼写、语法和写作风格建议。对辅助技术的支持已经过改进，可以访问此窗格。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p237">**Enhanced writing assistance with Editor pane:** Use the Editor pane for advanced spelling, grammar and writing style recommendations. ### <a name="word-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1163">Word：安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1163">Word: Security updates</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1166">[CVE-2018-0794](https://portal.msrc.microsoft.com/zh-CN/security-guidance/advisory/CVE-2018-0794)：Microsoft Word 远程代码执行漏洞</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1166">[CVE-2018-0794](https://portal.msrc.microsoft.com/zh-CN/security-guidance/advisory/CVE-2018-0794): Microsoft Word Remote Code Execution Vulnerability</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1181">修复了以下问题：如果运行 Windows 7 的计算机未安装 客户体验和诊断遥测更新，无法打开 Word。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1181">Fix an issue where Word won’t open on a computer running Windows 7 that doesn't have the update for customer experience and diagnostic telemetry installed.</span></span>

With this fix, user will now see an error message and the upload won't proceed.</span></span>

### <a name="excel-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1334">Excel：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1334">Excel: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1335">**“从示例中添加列”增强功能：** 支持更多的日期/时间、数学和索引列转换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1335">**“Add Column from Examples” enhancements:** Supports more Date/Time, Math, and Index Column transformations.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1336">**性能改进：** Excel 将以更快的速度打开包含多个工作表的复杂工作簿，以便可以更快地处理包含大片区域的公式、筛选多个行或进行复制和粘贴。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1336">**Performance improvements:** Excel opens complex workbooks with multiple sheets faster, so you can crunch formulas with large ranges, filter lots of rows, or copy and paste quicker.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1337">**插入联机图片：** 自动将图像插入用于选择图像和属性信息的新登录页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1337">**Insert online pictures:** New landing page for selecting images and attribution information is automatically inserted with the image.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1338">**Azure Data Lake Store 连接器：** 用户现在可以从 Azure Data Lake Store 导入数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1338">**Azure Data Lake Store connector:** Users can now import data from Azure Data Lake Store.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1339">**“从示例中添加列”增强功能：** 支持建议、更多的日期/时间操作和其他转换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1339">**"Add column from Examples" enhancements:** Supports suggestions, more Date/Time operations, and additional transformations.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1340">**“数据”选项卡**：“数据”选项卡上的功能区按钮已被重排到两个新组中：“获取和转换数据”以及“查询和连接”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1340">**Data tab**: Ribbon buttons on the Data tab have been rearranged into two new groups: Get & Transform Data and Queries & Connections.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1341">**共享查询**：可以将任意查询定义导出到 Office 数据库连接 (ODC) 文件中，然后跨工作簿共享或与其他人共享。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1341">**Share queries**: Export any query definition into an Office Database Connection (ODC) file, and then share it across workbooks or with others.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1342">**加载数据：** 可以将查询中的数据直接加载到数据透视表或数据透视图中，而无需将数据保存到数据模型中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1342">**Load data:** Load data from a query directly into PivotTables or PivotCharts without having to save the data into the Data Model.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1343">**共享文件活动：** 选择文件右上角的“活动”按钮，可以查看在 OneDrive for Business 或 SharePoint 中共享的文经共享、编辑、重命名或恢复的时间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1343">**Shared file activity:** Choose the Activity button in the upper right corner of the file to see when a file shared in OneDrive for Business or SharePoint was shared, edited, renamed, or restored.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p241">**安全链接：** 当用户单击链接时，Office 365 高级威胁防护 (ATP) 会检查此链接并判断它是否是恶意链接。如果认为此链接是恶意链接，则将用户重定向到警告页面而不是原始目标 URL。 [详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/dd6a1fef-ec4a-4cf4-a25a-bb591c5811e3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p241">**Safe links:** When a user clicks on a link, Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection (ATP) inspects the link to see if it’s malicious. If the link is deemed malicious, the user is redirected to a warning page instead of the original target URL. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/dd6a1fef-ec4a-4cf4-a25a-bb591c5811e3)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p242">**增强的数据导入功能：** 可从各种源轻松导入并形成数据。通过“查询和连接”侧窗格管理工作簿查询和连接，并通过 ODC 文件与他人共享查询。 [更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/ad78befd-eb1c-4ea7-a55d-79d1d67cf9b3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p242">**Enhanced data import functionality:** Easily import and shape data from various sources. Manage workbook queries and connections with the Queries & Connection side pane, and share queries with others via ODC files. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/ad78befd-eb1c-4ea7-a55d-79d1d67cf9b3)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-p243">**对共享文件做出的更改**：查看共享工作簿的更改人，并还原旧版工作簿。[更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/5c1e076f-a9c9-41b8-8ace-f77b9642e2c2)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-p243">**Changes in shared files**: View who has made changes in shared workbooks, and restore earlier versions. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/5c1e076f-a9c9-41b8-8ace-f77b9642e2c2)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1352">**含有笔按钮的套索选择：** 无需访问功能区，即可使用套索选择墨迹带的支持数字笔按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1352">**Lasso Select with a pen button:** Use supported digital pen buttons to Lasso Select ink without visiting the ribbon.</span></span>

### <a name="excel-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1364">Excel：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1364">Excel: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1365">修复了在编程创建数据透视表后，编程刷新导致 Excel 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1365">Fix an issue where the programmatic creation of a PivotTable followed by a programmatic refresh causes Excel to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1366">修复了在使用宏打开 Office 2007 或更低版本工作簿（.xls 或 .xla）时，用户错误地看到“灾难性故障”错误消息的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1366">Fix an issue where the user incorrectly sees a "catastrophic failure" error message when opening an Office 2007 or older workbook (.xls or .xla) with macros.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1368">修复了当文件名包含方括号时，用户无法在受保护视图中关闭工作簿的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1368">Fix an issue where the user can't close a workbook in protected view when the file name contains square brackets.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="dd90f-1369">修复了以下问题：当用户尝试在现有的工作簿中插入对象时，用户单击“浏览”导致 Excel 发生故障的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="dd90f-1369">Fix an issue where, when the user tries to insert an object in an existing workbook, Excel crashes when the user clicks Browse.</span></span>
